Revakhanda of the Vayupurana (RKV)
Based on the edition:
ørãkçùõadàs, Kùemràj (ed.): ørãskandamahàpuràõam. Veïkate÷vara Steam Press, Bombay: 1910.
and its reprint:
Siüha, Nàga÷araõa (ed.): ørãskandamahàpuràõam. pa¤cama bhàga: ÷rã àvantyakhaõóam. Nag Publishers, Delhi: 1986.


Input and proof-reading by Juergen Neuss, Freie Universitaet Berlin.
Proof-reading and corrections by Oliver Hellwig, Freie Universitaet Berlin.


NOTE BY THE CONTRIBUTOR:
The text has been wrongly assigned in the Veïkate÷vara edition 
(and subsequently) to the Skandapuràõa (i.e. SkP 5.3.); all available 
manuscriptual evidence, however, proves that the text was instead originally
part of the Vàyupuràõa. Nevertheless in the following text, the original 
colophones referring to the Skandapuràõa have been retained.
There is a Revàkhaõóa of the Skandapuràõa too, which, however, comprises 
116 adhyàyas only. That text is almost forgotten; I have also contributed 
an electronic version of that text to GRETIL.
(For further information on this group of texts, please contact the contributor at jneuss@arcor.de.)

|| iti  ÷rãskànde mahàpuràõa ekà÷ãtisàhasryàü saühitàyàü pa¤cama àvantyakhaõóe revàkhaõóe tãrthasaükhyàparigaõanavarõanaü nàmaikatriü÷adadhikadvi÷atatamo 'dhyàyaş ||
